\DoxyCodeLine{00028\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ Predicate\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ A\ function\ which\ takes\ one\ argument\ returns\ true\ if\ the\ argument\ meets\ some\ criteria.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00029\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ BinaryPredicate\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ A\ function\ which\ takes\ two\ arguments\ and\ returns\ true\ if\ some\ criteria\ is\ met\ (e.g.\ they\ are\ equal).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00030\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ StrickWeakOrdering\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ A\ BinaryPredicate\ that\ compares\ two\ objects,\ returning\ true\ if\ the\ first\ precedes\ the\ second.\ Like\ Compare\ but\ has\ additional\ requirements.\ Used\ for\ sorting\ routines.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00031\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ Function\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ A\ function\ which\ takes\ one\ argument\ and\ applies\ some\ operation\ to\ the\ target.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00032\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ Size\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ A\ count\ or\ size.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00033\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ Generator\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ A\ function\ which\ takes\ no\ arguments\ and\ returns\ a\ value\ (which\ will\ usually\ be\ assigned\ to\ an\ object).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00034\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ UnaryOperation\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ A\ function\ which\ takes\ one\ argument\ and\ returns\ a\ value\ (which\ will\ usually\ be\ assigned\ to\ second\ object).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00035\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ BinaryOperation\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ A\ function\ which\ takes\ two\ arguments\ and\ returns\ a\ value\ (which\ will\ usually\ be\ assigned\ to\ a\ third\ object).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00036\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ InputIterator\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ An\ input\ iterator\ (iterator\ you\ read\ from)\ which\ allows\ reading\ each\ element\ only\ once\ and\ only\ in\ a\ forward\ direction.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00037\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ ForwardIterator\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ An\ input\ iterator\ which\ is\ like\ InputIterator\ except\ it\ can\ be\ reset\ back\ to\ the\ beginning.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00038\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ BidirectionalIterator\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ An\ input\ iterator\ which\ is\ like\ ForwardIterator\ except\ it\ can\ be\ read\ in\ a\ backward\ direction\ as\ well.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00039\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ RandomAccessIterator\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ An\ input\ iterator\ which\ can\ be\ addressed\ like\ an\ array.\ It\ is\ a\ superset\ of\ all\ other\ input\ iterators.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00040\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ OutputIterator\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ An\ output\ iterator\ (iterator\ you\ write\ to)\ which\ allows\ writing\ each\ element\ only\ once\ in\ only\ in\ a\ forward\ direction.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00041\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00042\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Note\ that\ with\ iterators\ that\ a\ function\ which\ takes\ an\ InputIterator\ will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00043\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ also\ work\ with\ a\ ForwardIterator,\ BidirectionalIterator,\ or\ RandomAccessIterator.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00044\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ given\ iterator\ type\ is\ merely\ the\ -\/minimum-\/\ supported\ functionality\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00045\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ iterator\ must\ support.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00050\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Optimizations}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00051\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00052\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ There\ are\ a\ number\ of\ opportunities\ for\ optimizations\ that\ we\ take\ here}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00053\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ in\ this\ library.\ The\ most\ obvious\ kinds\ are\ those\ that\ subsitute\ memcpy}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00054\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ in\ the\ place\ of\ a\ conventional\ loop\ for\ data\ types\ with\ which\ this\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00055\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ possible.\ The\ algorithms\ here\ are\ optimized\ to\ a\ higher\ level\ than\ currently}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00056\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ available\ C++\ STL\ algorithms\ from\ vendors\ such\ as\ Microsoft.\ This\ is\ especially}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00057\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ so\ for\ game\ programming\ on\ console\ devices,\ as\ we\ do\ things\ such\ as\ reduce}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00058\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ branching\ relative\ to\ other\ STL\ algorithm\ implementations.\ However,\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00059\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ proper\ implementation\ of\ these\ algorithm\ optimizations\ is\ a\ fairly\ tricky}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00060\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ thing.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00061\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00062\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ various\ things\ we\ look\ to\ take\ advantage\ of\ in\ order\ to\ implement}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00063\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ optimizations\ include:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00064\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Taking\ advantage\ of\ random\ access\ iterators.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00065\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Taking\ advantage\ of\ trivially\ copyable\ data\ types\ (types\ for\ which\ it\ is\ safe\ to\ memcpy\ or\ memmove).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00066\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Taking\ advantage\ of\ type\_traits\ in\ general.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00067\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Reducing\ branching\ and\ taking\ advantage\ of\ likely\ branch\ predictions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00068\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Taking\ advantage\ of\ issues\ related\ to\ pointer\ and\ reference\ aliasing.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00069\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Improving\ cache\ coherency\ during\ memory\ accesses.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00070\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Making\ code\ more\ likely\ to\ be\ inlinable\ by\ the\ compiler.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00071\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
